Strategic Interpretation

Yunavaun Hollow Rebels won through an adaptive coastal forest approach because the result was decided by treasury, not territory, and their 7-point cash edge outweighed Rnutuan Tribe’s one-region lead. The board stayed unsettled across phases because different factions briefly led region counts, which meant no one converted map control into a decisive territorial break. Saklian Hollow Rebels’ early treasury edge mattered because it set the resource standard for the game, while Rnutuan’s stronger region position failed to convert into enough income to hold the finish.
The closest challenger was Rnutuan Tribe (Adaptive Forest Plains) at 142 treasury and 7 regions.

Victor's History

The Yunavaun Hollow Rebels prevailed by keeping their course steady when the map itself offered no easy certainty, finishing first on treasury with 149 despite conceding map share. Their Adaptive Coastal Forest approach was not the most expansive, but it was coherent: they opened actively, absorbed a mid-game setback, and still recovered to end with 6 regions and the strongest economy. By contrast, the Rnutuan Tribe’s larger territorial footprint could not quite convert into the same final advantage, and the late standings show that durable judgment mattered more than raw spread. In the end, this was a victory of disciplined adaptation and sound stewardship, not of reckless reach.
